[ISSUE-011] GROUP 4 - T002: Alarms Not Cancelled on Completion
=======================================================
Severity: HIGH (Data consistency)
Status: ‚úÖ FIXED (SESSION 10 CONTINUATION)

SYMPTOM:
User completes a todo (marks as done) but associated alarms still fire
User deletes a todo but alarms are orphaned in the database
Result: User gets alarmsfor tasks that no longer exist

INVESTIGATION:
TodoItem has toggleComplete() method ‚úÖ (sets completedAt timestamp correctly)
TodosBloc._onToggleTodo handler ‚úÖ (updates todo in DB and refreshes list)
BUT: No alarm cancellation logic in either handler

Alarms ARE linked to todos via linkedTodoId field (Alarm entity)
When todo is completed OR deleted ‚Üí no cleanup of linked alarms

ROOT CAUSE:
_onToggleTodo handler doesn't cancel alarms when todo.isCompleted changes
_onDeleteTodo handler doesn't cancel alarms before deleting todo

FIX APPLIED:
============

‚úÖ STEP 1: Enhanced _onToggleTodo handler
   File: lib/presentation/bloc/todos/todos_bloc.dart (lines 425-476)
   Change:
   - Check if todo is being marked complete: if (updatedTodo.isCompleted && !todo.isCompleted)
   - If yes: get all alarms, filter by linkedTodoId == todo.id
   - For each linked alarm: call alarmService.cancelNotification() + alarmRepository.deleteAlarm()
   - Graceful error handling: logs warning but doesn't fail the todo completion
   - Logs each cancelled alarm for debugging
   Status: ‚úÖ IMPLEMENTED & COMPILED

‚úÖ STEP 2: Enhanced _onDeleteTodo handler
   File: lib/presentation/bloc/todos/todos_bloc.dart (lines 483-537)
   Change:
   - When todo is deleted: get all alarms, filter by linkedTodoId == event.todoId
   - For each linked alarm: call alarmService.cancelNotification() + alarmRepository.deleteAlarm()
   - Before calling _todoRepository.deleteTodo()
   - Graceful error handling: logs warning but doesn't fail the deletion
   Status: ‚úÖ IMPLEMENTED & COMPILED

IMPACT OF FIX:
================
‚úÖ User completes todo ‚Üí alarms automatically cancelled
‚úÖ User deletes todo ‚Üí alarms automatically cleaned up
‚úÖ No orphaned alarms in database
‚úÖ Alarms list stays consistent with todo list
‚úÖ User doesn't get confused by alarms for completed/deleted tasks
‚úÖ Error handling is graceful (allearma cleanup failures are logged, not fatal)

TESTING CONSIDERATIONS:
=======================
- Mark todo complete, verify alarms disappear
- Delete todo, verify alarms disappear
- Check SQLite: deleted alarm records are removed
- Verify app continues if alarm service is temporarily unavailable

   - UpdateEndPositionEvent: Trim end point selection + validation

‚úÖ No repository depends on BLoCs

‚úÖ BLoCs never used as dependencies for services/repos

CURRENT IMPLEMENTATION:

‚úÖ What's handled:
  - Database initialization wrapped in try-catch in main.dart
  - AlarmService initialization wrapped in try-catch in DI setup
  - NotificationService initialization with proper error logging

‚ùå What's NOT handled:
  - No try-catch around the entire setupServiceLocator() call
  - No validation that all BLoCs are registered before use
  - If get<X>() called for unregistered X, throws without helpful message
  - No registration check before MultiRepositoryProvider/MultiBlocProvider
  - No assert(getIt.isRegistered<T>()) checks in critical paths

EXAMPLE ISSUE:
If a BLoC is not properly imported in injection_container.dart:
```
// Missing: getIt.registerFactory<ExampleBloc>(...);
// Later in main.dart:
// getIt<ExampleBloc>() throws: "No instance of ExampleBloc registered"
```
User sees generic error without context about what went wrong.

RECOMMENDED FIX (Optional enhancement):
```dart
Future<void> setupServiceLocator() async {
  try {
    AppLogger.i('Initializing Service Locator...');
    // ... all registrations ...
    AppLogger.i('‚úÖ All dependencies registered successfully');
  } catch (e) {
    AppLogger.e('CRITICAL: Service Locator setup failed: $e');
    rethrow; // Let main.dart handle crash
  }
}

// In main.dart, wrap setupServiceLocator():
try {
  await setupServiceLocator();
} catch (e) {
  print('FATAL: Failed to initialize app: $e');
  rethrow;
}
```

CURRENT STATUS: ‚úÖ FUNCTIONAL but not defensive

üî¥ **ML007: VideoPlaybackBloc ‚Äî No Resource Cleanup**
   Status: CRITICAL LEAK
   Issue: BLoC has NO close() method
   Problem: _onDisposeVideo() handler exists but is EMPTY (lines 92-96)
   Resource at risk: VideoPlayerController never disposed
   Impact: Memory leak when video player closed, device video resource not freed
   Recommendation: **IMPLEMENT IMMEDIATELY**
   Action: Add close() override with `_videoPlayerController?.dispose()`
   Location: lib/presentation/bloc/video_playback/video_playback_bloc.dart
   Severity: CRITICAL (affects device memory for video operations)

üî¥ **ML008: NoteEditorBloc ‚Äî No Listener Cleanup**
   Status: CRITICAL LEAK
   Issue: BLoC has NO close() method
   Problem: SpeechService initialized (line 29) but stopListening() only called on VoiceInputToggled event
   Resource at risk: Speech recognition listener runs indefinitely
   Impact: Memory leak + continuous background resource usage
   Scenario: User opens note editor, taps voice input once, then closes editor without voice input. Listener still active.
   Recommendation: **IMPLEMENT IMMEDIATELY**
   Action: Add close() override with `_speechService.stopListening()`
   Location: lib/presentation/bloc/note_editor/note_editor_bloc.dart
   Severity: CRITICAL (continuous background resource)

üî¥ **ML009: VoiceCommandService ‚Äî Singleton Never Disposed**
   Status: CRITICAL LEAK
   Issue: VoiceCommandService registered as SINGLETON in injection_container.dart (line 169)
   Problem: Service has NO close() or dispose() method
   Resource at risk: SpeechToText instance never disposed, initialization callbacks never cleared
   Impact: Singleton persists entire app lifetime with unreleased speech recognition resources
   Recommendation: **IMPLEMENT IMMEDIATELY**
   Action: 
   - Add dispose() method to VoiceCommandService
   - Call _speechToText.stop() and cleanup
   - In app shutdown (main.dart), call getIt<VoiceCommandService>().dispose()
   Location: lib/core/services/voice_command_service.dart
   Severity: CRITICAL (app-lifetime leak)

üî¥ **ML015: FocusSessionScreen ‚Äî No Lifecycle Cleanup**
   Status: CRITICAL LEAK
   Issue: StatefulWidget with NO dispose() method
   Problem: 
   - Wakelock enabled in build() (line 30: `Wakelock.enable()`)
   - No corresponding Wakelock.disable() in cleanup
   - Screen has 946 lines but ZERO resource cleanup
   Resource at risk: Screen lock held even after navigator.pop()
   Impact: Screen stays on indefinitely after focus session ends
   Recommendation: **IMPLEMENT IMMEDIATELY**
   Action:
   - Add dispose() override
   - Call `Wakelock.disable()` to restore normal screen lock behavior
   - Close any focus-related streams
   Location: lib/presentation/pages/focus_session_screen.dart (line 28-100)
   Severity: CRITICAL (UX-breaking: device never sleeps)

üî¥ **ML017: ReflectionHomeScreen ‚Äî No Lifecycle Cleanup**
   Status: CRITICAL LEAK
   Issue: StatefulWidget with NO dispose() method
   Problem:
   - LocalAuthentication instance created (line 27) but never cleaned up
   - Future.delayed() with no cancellation mechanism (line 59-66)
   - Timer in initState() with no cleanup
   Resource at risk: Delayed futures and authentication listeners persist
   Impact: Memory leak from uncancelled futures, authentication locks remain
   Recommendation: **IMPLEMENT IMMEDIATELY**
   Action:
   - Add dispose() override
   - Cancel any pending futures
   - Clean up LocalAuthentication listeners
   Location: lib/presentation/pages/reflection_home_screen.dart (line 27-100)
   Severity: CRITICAL (futures block cleanup)

   Status: CRITICAL - Already Fixed (Session 13)
   Problem: Was calling _initFocusScreen() inside build() method
   Impact: 
   - Timer restarted on EVERY rebuild
   - Events (LoadNotesEvent, SelectTaskEvent) dispatched on every rebuild
   - Pure build method violation
   
   ‚úÖ RESOLUTION ALREADY APPLIED:
   - Converted from StatelessWidget ‚Üí StatefulWidget
   - Moved _initFocusScreen() from build() ‚Üí initState()
   - Events now dispatched only ONCE when screen created, not on rebuild
   Location: lib/presentation/pages/focus_session_screen.dart (previously fixed)
   Current Status: ‚úÖ FIXED

‚ö†Ô∏è **SE002: EnhancedRemindersListScreen ‚Äî Side Effects in build()**

   - Side effects correctly moved to initState(), NOT called from build()

   Location: lib/presentation/pages/enhanced_reminders_list_screen.dart
   Current Status: ‚úÖ VERIFIED CLEAN
